@​everyone I have an update regarding the server's login procedure
The console activation error (23888) has been disabled temporarily to allow new players to connect easier to CoWFC
While on the back-end console activation procedures have not changed, new users should no longer get an error code
New consoles will continue to populate in the admin panel for activation
What this means is people can go nuts with MAC changers, which is unfortunate
